            <script language="JavaScript" type="text/javascript">
                function togglePriceSearch() {
                  if(document.getElementById('home_price_block').style.display == "block") {
                  document.getElementById('home_price_block').style.display = "none";
                  document.getElementById('monthly_payment_block').style.display = "block";
                  } else {
                  document.getElementById('home_price_block').style.display = "block";
                  document.getElementById('monthly_payment_block').style.display = "none";
                  }
                }
                // ensure we are searching by listing price OR monthly_payment
                function adjustPriceCriteria(form) {
                  if(form.monthly_payment_min) {
                  if(document.getElementById('home_price_block').style.display == "block") {
                  form.monthly_payment_min.value = "";
                  form.monthly_payment_max.value = "";
                  } else {
                  form.listing_price_min.value = "";
                  form.listing_price_max.value = "";
                  }
                  }

                  return true;
                }
            </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
  
  function saveHome(id, mlsNumber, mlsSource) {
    var _gaq = _gaq || [];
    _gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'save_home', 'complete', '']);
    var success = function(o) {
      var i = parseInt(o.responseText);
      if(i == -2) {
        alert("You have 100 saved homes.  Please remove homes before adding more."); // todo: overlay
      } else if(i == -1) {
        alert("You must be a registered user to save homes.  Please register and try again."); // todo: overlay
      } else if(i > 0) {
        var elem = document.getElementById(id);
        if(elem) {
          elem.innerHTML = '<span></span>Saved';
          YAHOO.util.Dom.addClass(elem, "active");
          if(elem.href) {
            elem.href = _JSP_URL_PREFIX + "/account/my_homes/austin/detailed.jsp"; // todo: pass in the metro
          }
        }
      }
      //alert("success: " + o.responseText);
    };
    var failure = function(o) {
      //alert("failure: " + o.responseText);
    };

    var callback = {
      success: success,
      failure: failure
    };
    var url = '/xhr/saveHome?cxp=1&mlsNumber=' + mlsNumber + '&mlsSource=' + mlsSource;
    //  alert(url);
    YAHOO.util.Connect.asyncRequest('POST', url, callback);
  }
  
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
  function saveAddress(id, addressId) {
    var _gaq = _gaq || [];
    _gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'save_address', 'complete', '']);

      } else if(i > 0) {
        var elem = document.getElementById(id);
        if(elem) {
          elem.innerHTML = '<span></span>Watching';
          YAHOO.util.Dom.addClass(elem, "active");
          if(elem.href) {
            elem.href = _JSP_URL_PREFIX + "/account/my_homes/austin/detailed.jsp"; // todo: pass in the metro
          }
        }
      }
      //alert("success: " + o.responseText);
    };
    var failure = function(o) {
      //alert("failure: " + o.responseText);
    };

      success: success,
      failure: failure
    };

<script type="text/javascript">
  
  function requestPhotoNotification(id, mlsNumber, mlsSource) {

    var success = function(o) {
      var elem = document.getElementById(id);
      if(elem) {
        elem.innerHTML = 'We\'ll notify you when a photo becomes available.';
      }
      //alert("success: " + o.responseText);
    };
    var failure = function(o) {
      //alert("failure: " + o.responseText);
    };

    var callback = {
      success: success,
      failure: failure
    };
    var url = '/xhr/requestPhotoNotification?mlsNumber=' + mlsNumber + '&mlsSource=' + mlsSource;
    //  alert(url);
    YAHOO.util.Connect.asyncRequest('POST', url, callback);
  }
  
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
  
  function likeHome(id,  mlsNumber, mlsSource, isLike) {
    var _gaq = _gaq || [];
  _gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'like_home', 'complete', '']);

    var success = function(o) {
      var elem = document.getElementById(id);
      if(elem) {
        if(isLike) {
          elem.innerHTML = parseInt(elem.innerHTML) + 1;
        } else {
          elem.innerHTML = parseInt(elem.innerHTML) - 1;
        }
      }
      //alert("success: " + o.responseText);
    };
    var failure = function(o) {
      //alert("failure: " + o.responseText);
    };

    var callback = {
      success: success,
      failure: failure
    };
    var url = '/xhr/likeHome?mlsNumber=' + mlsNumber + '&mlsSource=' + mlsSource + '&isLike=' + isLike;
    //  alert(url);
    YAHOO.util.Connect.asyncRequest('POST', url, callback);
  }
  
</script>

function showComments(counter) { 
 document.getElementById('comments_trunc_' + counter).style.display = 'none';
 document.getElementById('comments_all_' + counter).style.display = 'block';
}
function hideComments(counter) { 
 document.getElementById('comments_trunc_' + counter).style.display = 'block';
 document.getElementById('comments_all_' + counter).style.display = 'none';
}

  <script type="text/javascript">

    function actionStripWidget(obj){

      this.obj = obj;
      this.stripElem = YAHOO.util.Selector.query(".actionBoxStrip",this.obj, true);
      this.animateIn =  new YAHOO.util.Anim(this.stripElem, {opacity: {  to: 1 }}, .3);
      this.animateOut =  new YAHOO.util.Anim(this.stripElem, {opacity: {  to: 0 }}, .3);


      YAHOO.util.Event.addListener(this.obj, "mouseenter", this.fadeIn, this, true);
      YAHOO.util.Event.addListener(this.obj, "mouseleave", this.fadeOut, this, true);

    }


    actionStripWidget.prototype.fadeIn = function(){
      stripElem = this.stripElem;
      this.animateIn.onComplete.subscribe( function(){
         YAHOO.util.Dom.addClass(stripElem, "sans_trans");
      });
      this.animateIn.animate();
    };
    actionStripWidget.prototype.fadeOut = function(){
      stripElem = this.stripElem;
      YAHOO.util.Dom.removeClass(stripElem, "sans_trans");
      this.animateOut.animate();
    };

    Z.addOnLoadEventHandler(function(){
      var tmp = YAHOO.util.Selector.query('div.homebox', 'ccinnerbox');
      for(i= 0; i<tmp.length; i++){
         new actionStripWidget(tmp[i]);
      }
    });



</script>
